God's Homeland
I sincerely thank you all for your congratulations. I deeply apologize for limiting the attendance of all Unification Church members around the world, or those within the United States, on this day of celebration. One thing I hope you remember is that we are in the midst of a war that centers on God's will. I hope you will recognize this again. 
Make this day a stepping stone for progress
I hope that you will take this day as an opportunity to commit to progress, and that is why I took such measures, so I ask for your understanding. Furthermore, I am especially grateful to all the members who are sending me congratulatory messages from overseas at this time, whether they know me or not, and to the countless people from various countries who are offering their sincere prayers and blessings.
People in the world generally like to have more of one thing. Most people think this way. Those who have one want to have two, and those who have two think it's something to boast about to have three.
Now, what do you think about getting older? Those who like it are immature. Even if we consider children and young teenagers in their twenties as exceptions, as people come to know the world and their responsibilities and duties become heavier, and as they bear historical responsibilities, getting older is not something good; rather, it is a solemn and sad thing, isn't it? Most people think this way. (Laughter)
Now, my age is considered a "Hwangap" in Korea. There is a set trajectory of 60 years. To surpass that stage… When I think back to my childhood, around 7 or 8 years old, I remember that when elders in the neighborhood reached their sixtieth birthday, they were celebrated. At that time in Korea, we would sing traditional Korean music, call in entertainers, and enjoy ourselves, and while we enjoyed that song, the elders would think, "Ah, now they are starting to go down the hill towards death." They thought that way, and I too thought, "Ah, that person is not far from death." (Laughter) That was just the other day, and now I have already become that age. Isn't that right? (Cheers and applause)
Now, when I think about this, I believe that Unification Church members will gradually stop having expectations and hopes for me. I think we are entering a stage where that may no longer be necessary. "No, that's not true." Yes, it is! "No, that's not true!" Oh, that's fine. I agree with you. (Laughter)
When I quietly think about Reverend Moon of the Unification Church, I believe that people in the world think this way. Outsiders might think, "I hope that person ages quickly and dies so that there will be no issues with immigration, no issues with the State Department, and no problems within the United States." Most people would think like that. There are all kinds of people, with all kinds of thoughts, and all sorts of miscellaneous characters. However, Unification Church members are not miscellaneous. They are one group. They look alike, walk the same path, and behave in similar ways. These young members do not like the fact that their teacher is getting older, and they might think, "Oh, it would be nice if he could start subtracting a year from his age starting from 60." (Applause)
11 
Then, putting aside the world, what would God think? God sent Reverend Moon into the world, and from a young age, he has faced insults, been chased from his country, chased from Asia, chased from the world, and suffered hardships wherever he went. If that was not for his own benefit but for God, would God think, "Oh, I feel sorry for making him suffer for 60 years, so I should bring him back quickly as he gets older"? Or would God think, "It would be better if he suffers more in the world and comes back having taken more responsibility for the complexities of the world"? What do you think? How do you think God would feel? "Second." You don't know, do you? A loving parent does not want their child to suffer. That is why they want to quickly relieve their child from suffering and have them by their side.
But the spirits of the Unification Church, the spiritual beings, are the opposite. They would say, "Oh, it would be nice if he could live longer and suffer more with us." They would want him to suffer more, more. What does that mean? It means they want him to suffer to the point of death. "No, that's not true." I don't know about that. I think that way. (Laughter)
Now, you may think that way, but one thing that remains is how my mother and my children would think. (Laughter) They probably wouldn’t think like you. They would think, "Since he has suffered all this time, we should take care of him comfortably and let him enjoy life centered around family." This lingering thought might exist. Therefore, it would be difficult for God as well.
So, what do you think, Reverend Moon? I have no lingering desire to live a long life. I know well what the spiritual world is like, so I have no desire to live long in this world. So what do you think? Now that I have started this work, I am in the process. The democratic world does not know where it is heading in the future. It does not know what will happen to the communist world either. The only person on this planet who knows these issues centered on God's will is Reverend Moon. 
12 
It is not about what will happen thousands of years later; it is that the time is not long. The time is not long. Therefore, the world will continue to plunge into a downward trend. So, what will happen to the Unification Church when the teacher is gone? What will happen to the members of the Unification Church? When they are exhausted from fighting, they might look to the teacher for strength, but if the teacher is not on the earth, it will be overwhelming. However, even if I grow old, as long as I remain on earth, I can still instruct you on what to do and how to act. Do you think that is necessary? 
"Yes." You have received guidance from the teacher your whole life, but if I grow old, what will happen? Even if you dislike it, if you realize that the world needs me, you must overcome that, I think. However, the older I get, the more health becomes an issue, and energy becomes an issue, and I will be different from young people…. I am at a busier time now than when I was young; how will I handle this? Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
Always be ahead of the spiritual world that works 24 hours
Now, if we put the teacher at the forefront, while the teacher leads, should you help him, or should you pull him back? Should you push him or pull him? "We should push." So, will you push alone, or will you push together as a nation, or will you push together with all humanity? How will you push? "Together with all humanity." Now, what about the spiritual world? Will the spirits also push the teacher, or not? Who do you think will push first? Will the young people of the Unification Church take the lead in pushing, or will the spirits of the spiritual world take the lead? "The young people of the Unification Church." I think so too. (Laughter) That is the issue.
One thing you must think about is that the spiritual world works 24 hours without rest. You need to understand that it transcends time and space. Do spirits in the spiritual world need time to sleep? "No." Think about that. How incredible is that? Would that be good or bad? "Good." What is good about it? Why?
When people are having fun and are excited, sometimes sleeping and eating become bothersome. If that state continues, there is no need to think about sleep. Do you have such serious matters? Do you have such matters? Is there something serious enough that you can go beyond time, beyond sleep, and beyond play? "Yes." Is there someone here who is fundraising, someone who is going out to evangelize? Is there someone doing home church? Is that the case or not? That is why they are losing. Would saying this make you feel uncomfortable? "Today, on the teacher's birthday, I should say something good, but here I am being made to wear a hat." (Laughter) If you only listen to me, I will take it off for you, right? I have to take it off. The teacher knows the way to go in the short term.
Now, when you enter this short term, you must not think about sleep or anything else. You must go swiftly. At that time, you must tighten your tie and pull this thing along. (Demonstrating) Do you want that? "Yes." If the teacher is old and weak, would it be okay to attach an electric motor here to create strong arms and legs to push and pull? "Yes." Thank you very much. (Laughter) I promised, right? "Yes." Now it is done.
So today, I have one thing to say…. This ceiling is saying, "They don't recognize me." (Laughter) For the first time in the world, I was born through the efforts of the Unification Church, and I am the most honored guest here today, but it is unfortunate that they do not recognize me. Therefore, I should say, "Thank you, ceiling." (Laughter, applause)
14   
In the future, such works will be…. The teacher's vision has been greatly incorporated. (Applause) In that sense, when the teacher goes to the spiritual world and you all grow old, and the second generation begins to move this world, this place will become a place revered more than any palace. Especially considering that this place was prepared with such care and effort to celebrate the teacher's 60th birthday, it will become a place of longing for many people. At that time, there will be no carpet. This wooden floor and ceiling will become friends of tears for all people, descendants, and friends of the heart, and will also become a fence for the source of future strength. 
The natural is the sacred
Now, first, on this truly joyful day, how will you celebrate when you see this? Will you lose to the future generations? "No, we will not." You should open your eyes wide (making a gesture) and look like this. (Laughter) Such thoughts are necessary. This is the best time to talk about such things. Serious talk is not necessary, right? Serious talk is not necessary. "No, it is not."
Oh, it has already been 30 minutes. It has been 28 minutes. Today, I should take a break. Speaking is really hard. I will talk later, so let’s stop now. "No, we will not." Who decides that? I will stop now. "No, it cannot be." (The audience claps in rhythm, indicating they want more words.) I understand, so you want me to speak? "Yes." Then, should I…. (Laughter) Should I drink some water?
Now, has your heart relaxed a bit? Is there anyone here who is seeing the teacher for the first time? There shouldn’t be, right? There shouldn’t be. Oh, is there someone who has not attended? "The missionaries." The missionaries have all seen the teacher before, right? "No, they are the missionaries brought from the field." You all are people who went out as missionaries in Germany or the United States and have not seen the teacher, right? "Yes, that is correct." Then I apologize. How does the teacher look to you? 
15 
Is he ugly? "No." (Laughter) When you only see photos, you might think that our teacher flies up to the second floor, does not need to go to the bathroom, does not use chopsticks, and when he says, "Hey, come in, rice," it just flows in, right? (Laughter) You might think he does not need to go to the bathroom…. Didn’t you think that? Didn’t you? Isn’t it true that what is natural is sacred? The chirping of birds is sacred, the flying of butterflies is sacred, the sound of the blowing wind, the sound of the typhoon, the sound of thunder—all of that is sacred. Do you understand?
So, a person blinks their eyes, moves their hands, breathes, and must love. The teacher also has tears, sadness, pain, and difficulties, but those are more extreme than yours. If the breadth is wider, it is seen as wider. So, if it is severe, it is severe, and if it is merciless, it is merciless, and if it is good, that conclusion comes from there. Do you understand what I mean? If such things fit into the natural principles and the rhythm of the universe, then it is great and sacred. I would like to talk about such things today, but since it is time for the principle lecture, I will stop here. Do you understand?
The emergence of numerous countries on Earth is the result of numerous struggles
Now, knowing that, let’s talk. What should we talk about today? Let’s hear some titles from you. Depending on the titles you mention, let’s talk. There cannot be a more joyful day than this. Where should we talk? Let’s talk. One by one. "Change of heart," "Testimony of the Father," "Testimony of the Mother," "How far is restoration?" "The relationship between the Father and God." Now, look. All of those can exist. Is there something we do not have? What do we not have? "There is no Mother's Day." (Laughter, applause) Mother's Day is included in Parents' Day.
Now, do we have no money? We have money, right? Do we have no people? How many people are there? What do we lack? What do we not have? Is there anything we do not possess? God speaks, right? Is there no money, no strength, or no people? We have everything, right? What is it that we lack?

So, when that news spreads, there will be those who say, "Well done!" and others who will feel sorry for him. This is not just someone else's story; it is your story. 

When that happens, the people who are waiting for the opportunity to attack will say, "Let’s get him!" and will gather together. They will think, "We can take him down." But there will also be those who will say, "No, we shouldn't do that." 

This is the reality of human relationships. When you look at the world, it is full of these kinds of conflicts. 

Now, let’s think about how we can overcome this. The way to overcome it is to love our enemies. If we can love our enemies, we can create a world where peace can exist. 

This is the essence of the message that Jesus brought. He taught us to love our enemies, to pray for those who persecute us. 

If we can embody this teaching, we can create a new world, a world that God desires. 

So, what is the conclusion? The conclusion is that we must love our enemies. 

This is not just a simple saying; it is a profound truth that can change the course of history. 

If we can love our enemies, we can break down the barriers that divide us. 

We can create a world where nations do not fight against each other, where people do not hate each other. 

This is the vision that we must strive for. 

We must work together to create a world where love prevails over hatred, where understanding prevails over conflict. 

This is the path that God is calling us to walk. 

So let us take this message to heart and live it out in our lives. 

Let us be the ones who love our enemies and work towards a world of peace. 

This is the calling of our time, and we must rise to meet it.

I'm afraid it seems like it will be difficult. Then what do you have? If strength doesn't work, what do you have next? What do you fill it with? If you fill it with things, then you have to fill it with all kinds of things. Then would that vessel be good? "No, it wouldn't." So, in that vessel, what is it that is good for both here and there when you fill it up with all your might, whether suddenly or however? "True love!" (laughter) I don't know, but true love! That sounds good. When we talk about true love, no matter how serious we are, when it comes to true love, we bow down and just talk about true love... Love is the only thing that can cover the universe.
So, let's think about whether true love can fill everything or not. Look at this hand of mine; look at your hands. This little thing is trying to scratch, this hand of mine. (laughter) It rarely reaches out. It doesn't move. Also, look at the mouth. This mouth doesn't move. And look at the eyes, like a snake's eyes... Also, look at the ears. It hears, but... This leg doesn't want to move. It's just like this. (laughter) 

Even if you offer money, it thinks about it; even if you study, it thinks about it; even if you give knowledge, it thinks about it; even if you give power, it thinks about it. Everything goes back and forth, complicatedly. However, if you give the injection of love, that unifies everything at once. So, those who walk the path of love have their eyes like this, and everything is not stiff but loosened up like this. No matter how ugly we may look, everything opens the door. It opens the door 180 degrees. In that, all actions become unified.

If we have the five senses, think of it as 'the five-sense tank, the five-sense tank is passing by.' (drawing while speaking) Think of it as a tank. Where does it go? It doesn't go haphazardly; it goes swiftly to one place. Think about how fast that would be. And then it comes from the other person, whether it's a woman or a man. If that is fast, there is nothing faster in the world, and if it is big, there is nothing bigger, and if it is good, there is nothing better. It explodes. 'Boom'—this explosion phenomenon occurs. When it happens all at once, where does it all go? Do they exist? They all become disoriented. "No, they don't."

When you look at it this way, if all the cells are unified and can explode and shine brightly, what would that be? It is love. No matter how much you think about it, the only thing that can act like that is love. There is nothing but love. If there are five senses, then there must be a blanket for the five senses; it would be this kind of blanket that could cover the universe... You can't make that in the world with gold or anything else. The only thing that can be made is love. It becomes a blanket made of love, a wrapping, a bed. 

Think about what color that is. Would it be a good color or a bad color? "It's a good color." The more you think about it, the more it becomes a good color. Combining those five colors creates a swirling core. There is a center.

When I went to Vietnam, when the husband returns from the army, there must be a center where you go to the airport or the dock to hold onto him. At that time, the man is the center, and the woman runs and lifts her legs... That can't be helped. She's short. (laughter) Everyone would have been like that. The swirling of the universe, when the wrapping of love spins and swirls, that center is ideal. That is the ideal.

When you combine seven colors of light, it becomes white light, right? Regardless of the past, when it returns with the power of love, will that light be bright red or white? When you combine and rotate the seven colors of light, it becomes white light. Why is it white light? It means that when anything is exchanged quickly, it becomes white. 

Do you understand? Just because white people are good at giving and receiving everything doesn't mean they are white. (laughter) In this way, regardless of ancestors, colors are mixed, and all kinds of lights come out, but wrapped in this love, it spins around... How beautiful would that be? When you see that, think about how surprised you would be, opening your mouth and saying 'Ah—' in admiration.

Humans are beings born from love.
So then, where do we humans come from? Where were humans born? Where was I born? I was born from this action and this movement. (drawing while speaking) Do you want to be born here or there? "From the center." You have many desires. (laughter)

When you look at it this way, where were people born? They were born from the love of their parents. I was born from the love of my parents, and I was born as the central owner of that love. You must understand this. I am the central owner of love. What of love? "The center."

Even though the mother and father loved each other, life arose, so that life is the center. Life is the center. The life of the mother and the life of the father are connected around 'me.' Finally, it bore fruit. The mother is not the center, and the father is not the center; I am the center. You must understand that I am the center as the essence of the combined lives of my mother and father. Do you understand what that means? "Yes." The love of the mother and the love of the father is not the center; I am the center. The mother is external, and the father is external, but because of me, the result was born from their oneness, so I was born as the center of love.

Then, who did the mother and father start loving for? It was not for themselves. It concludes that it was for me. This movement happened because of me. To bring forth just me... That's why when I go, my mother and father are drawn to me. As long as they hold the string of love, they are drawn to me.

Because of that authority, I can assert my rights equally centered around my father and mother. "Father and mother are unhappy without me. They can only be happy if I exist." At that time, my father and mother say, "That's right." And I also say that I would be unhappy without my mom and dad. Why is that? Because the parents are the cause, and I am the result. We are one. The cause and the result become one, forming the body of love. This is the principle of the universe. Do you understand? "Yes."

In our principle, it is said that when the subject and object become one, power emerges. Here, there is power. (drawing while speaking) Then, when the cause, the mother and father, become one with me, because the subject and object have become one, a new subject can become one. If God exists, and if we become completely one centered on God's ideal love, we become completely in a subject-object relationship with God. When the complete love rights of the ideal son-in-law between God and humanity are realized, there will always be light in the universe, shining like the bright sun of love.

Everyone, the principle of motors or electricity... (drawing while speaking) It works like this, right? This one is attracted, and this one repels; it must work like this to turn. Do you understand? "Yes." The universe is turning. Therefore, just as power emerges continuously and exponentially, when it starts to turn with love, the universe will be filled with ideal power. Time has passed a lot. What time did we start? "6 o'clock." What time did we start? "6:10."

So then, where did my journey start? "Love." From fighting, from fighting? "No." Then from what? "Love." Right, when you touch it, does it taste like love? "Yes." (laughter) Talking about children, when you see your parents, you just hug them, suck on them, and even if they poop, they are not ugly but cute, and whatever they do, even if they drool, it is not unpleasant but delicious. Isn't that strange? (laughter) Why is that? "Love." Love, love is there.

Seeing that baby is a reaction of your own love once again. It raises your love again, exploding the actions that originally took place. So, the mother and father dive into the baby, and the baby tries to dive into the mother and father. Nowadays, in America, women are trying not to breastfeed. However, they should breastfeed. Breastfeeding is connecting a pipe to their body, supplying everything like a hose. (laughter) They like it while supplying it. They enjoy giving. And the baby enjoys drinking.

Born from the oneness of my parents' love.
So when you think about it, when you think that you were born in this universe of love, do you think it was worth being born? Was it good to be born, or would it have been better not to be born? "It was good to be born." How happy are you? "Very happy." Are you crazy happy? (laughter) So, in the world, can you boast about being born? Can you boast about it? "Yes." How much can you boast about it? How much can you boast about it?

While thinking about that, when you say, "Hey, I became like this, so why do you ignore me?" that resonates. "Oh, I was like that. I didn't know." That comes out. Regarding God, "God, you didn't make me to be born as this core that moves in this love of five colors. God, who says love is the best, can you ignore me?" At that time, "Hmm, I like you," is what happens. I was the ideal, explosive discovery that God was researching in the laboratory. It is life. Therefore, destroying this is the greatest sin, and loving and protecting it is the greatest good; this conclusion emerges.

So, suicide is the greatest sin. It is a malicious act to destroy the universe. Such a person must go to the hell of hells. Is there anyone among you who wants to commit suicide? Raise your hand if you have thought about wanting to commit suicide. There must be many. Raise your hand. This fact, knowing it, now listening to the teacher, can you think, "Hey, I can't commit suicide"? "No." That's why it's necessary to come here early in the morning and receive education without letting you sleep. (applause)

So, who am I? I must know that I am the connection of my parents' lives. I am the connection of life. I am the union of the two lives of my father and mother. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, I am not separate; I follow wherever I go. I am connected. I am bound by an invisible string. Also, who am I? I am a participant in love. I am the oneness of my parents' love. I am in unity of love.

Next, who am I? I am the oneness of happiness, the ideal, the oneness of my parents' ideals. Everything is included. It is all one. What is the ideal? It includes happiness and everything. It includes peace and everything. For parents, in the world, they try to succeed, to be happy, but when they meet a lost child, the joy of that is incomparable to the joy of their own success. There is no comparison. Therefore, it is the highest ideal, the oneness of ideals.

So, who are you? The lifeline of your mother and father is attached to you. Do you understand what that means? "Yes." Next, the string of love is attached to you. Then, the string of your parents' ideals is attached. Who can cut this? Not even God can cut it, nor can the universe; no one can cut it. It is best to leave it as it is. All the power of the universe wants to support that. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, thinking of your parents as your own body, loving your parents, and being filial to your parents is the most brilliant thing for humans. Why? Why is that? When this becomes powerful and shines like plus and minus in electricity, the whole universe pays attention. Everything comes running. It shines, it shines. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Blessings come to harmonious families. This saying is all because of that.

The divorce of parents is like cutting a child in half with a knife. The laws of the universe do not allow that. Parents who go against this will face disaster wherever they go, and there can be no happiness anywhere. From this perspective, the conclusion is that divorce is impossible. Raise your hand if your mother and father are living apart. Put your hands down. Doesn't it feel like you have been cut in half with a saw? Doesn't it feel good? "No, it doesn't." That's right. That's why America is failing. It will fail. America must fail. It is a sign of rapid failure.

The three generations of parents who gave birth to me.
Now, how long will it take to talk like this? Let's jump. "No." I got it.

Even if you go to Korea from here, your parents will follow you, right? Even in the spirit world, they follow you everywhere. Your parents always follow you. Our Yejin follows too. (laughs) Therefore, to say, "Oh, my mother and father..." and to dislike that is the greatest sin. You must understand that it is a destructive thing to cause chaos in the universe. To dislike this means that person is already going down the path of decline. This is a path that goes against principles and laws. It is the principle to take your parents with you as you rise. Do you understand? "Yes."

The reason your eyes are alive is not because you are alive, but because of your parents. You are still growing well. You are growing for yourself, but you are growing for your parents. Thank you, parents, how about that? "Thank you." This is something only taught in the Unification Church. (applause) To talk about this would take several books, but it's hard to do it in a short time.

So then, talking about parents, how many parents do I have? To be born, I went through my parents, but how many parents gave birth to me? Is it one or a complex? Singular or plural? I knew about myself, but I went through my parents, so how many parents gave birth to me? "Three." (laughter) That's right.

So, what is the first? The world of matter. All cells are matter; matter. You must understand that all matter is our first parent. Do you understand? That matter itself, the elements themselves, are the ancestors that gave birth to you. This matter rests and settles only in the position of love and ideals. The universe is made so that all cells can comfortably live only in the position of love and ideals. When you get angry, everything twists and turns.
You all came from matter. This extension is the world of matter. I think that I was formed as a complex being, with the essence of matter extracted from the world of matter. 

Then who is next? It is my parents who gave birth to me. They shaped me into a form that allowed me to become who I am. However, no matter how much they try, parents cannot be the masters of love. They can be the masters of my life, but they cannot be the masters of love. This is something you need to understand.

So, who is the master of love? The reason we need God is to universalize love, to eternalize love. Eternal love... Do you understand? "Yes." Because God is the subject of love, He becomes a parent centered around love. Do you understand? Therefore, we have three generations of parents.

From this perspective, what is the time in the womb? It is the time when matter is leaping forward. Do you understand? "Yes." It is the time when I grow, receiving the supply of matter from my parents. It is the time when I live in the embrace of my parents. It is the inner sanctuary within the realm of material love. It sounds strange to say material love, but that’s what it is. They provide everything. They give birth to me by forming 'me.' Do you understand? "Yes."

Then comes the time of birth. The time in the womb lasts ten months, the physical life lasts a hundred years, and the spiritual life lasts thousands and tens of thousands of years. (While writing on the board) So we spend ten months in the womb before being born. After receiving all the material supply, when we are fully formed, we come out from the embrace of the first parent into the embrace of the second parent, which is birth.

Now, what happens during this time? The parents take responsibility for my human supply; I must become a person. They provide everything about what a person is. They supply me with what kind of person I should be, living in the world where the parents exist. Education and everything else is a life of receiving supply centered around the parents. It is the time of birth. It is the parents who provide. It is the parents' nation, the parents' world that provides. Everything is supplied through the parents. Do you understand? "Yes." They represent the world, and then they represent the nation within the world, and they represent the family within the nation, and they provide everything for the whole. [Prayer]
Beloved Father, before your glorious will to block the flow of history and establish the shield of victory, we once again kneel down and apologize for the shame of our ancestors in the past. From the history of sin from Adam and Eve until it affects countless humans today, you have carried this burden for countless eons, fighting in the darkness of twists and turns that no one knows, and when we think about this fact, Father, we truly feel ashamed before your hard work. This humanity, these descendants of the fall, would be worthy of being abandoned a million times, but because you are the creative subject who cannot abandon them, we realize that you have come this far following the path of restoration based on the principle.

In that process, countless people have come and gone, and many have passed through this land in the twists of struggle and sorrow, but when they go to the spirit world, they remain in the sorrow of history that cannot hide their shame before you, groaning beneath the limits of your ideals. No one could comfort your heart, which could not be joyful whether looking at the earth or the sky, and there was not a single son who could be a companion to your heart, to call you the subject and share their stories with you, nor a single daughter.

Furthermore, Father, there was no parent who could boast that your love is like this, and there were no beloved children before their parents. The Rough Road of Death

Today's sermon title is 'The Rough Road of Death.' What does that mean? It is the path of purpose. 

The tears, blood, and sweat in history exist because humanity has fallen. 

Among all the people living in today's world, there is not a single person, regardless of gender, who wishes to take a difficult or thorny path. This is true for individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world as a whole. So what kind of path do they want to take? They want a smooth path, a flat road like a highway. No one wants to drive on a highway that goes through a desert. They want to drive on a highway with beautiful scenery. 

In general, in the East, the path of life is often expressed in terms of roads. Happy paths, unhappy paths, paths of peace—there are many expressions involving the word 'road.' 

When we look at this, the question of why it has become this way is a serious issue. No one wants to go the opposite way. This is true not only for humans but also for nature. All of nature is the same. Grass does not want to live a hard life; it wants to grow vigorously in good soil. Animals and birds are the same; they all want to live in places that are abundant and comfortable. 

So, if all beings in the world want such a path, what is the cause of them going down a different path? And if there is a God who created all things, what would God want? God also wants the same thing, so why has it turned out this way? From this perspective, we can deduce that humanity has gone wrong; something is wrong. 

If we look again, did historical figures live lives of tears or lives of joy? All the revered historical figures and saints were people who shed tears, blood, and sweat. Did they do this willingly, or were they compelled by some external force? Even if they wanted to, they felt a responsibility to overcome the evil of their nation or the social systems of their time, which were bad, and they had to take such positions amid the adversities of society. They walked that path to overcome their unhappy circumstances. 

From this perspective, we can conclude that all those who have woven history and developed it into a new history have walked the path of tears, blood, and sweat. 

So where does happiness start? What is the starting point of happiness? Where do peace and our ideals as humans begin? Will they start from crossing the hill of tears and blood and sweat, or will they start before that? That is the question. What do you think? "They start after crossing." Why after crossing? Why is that? This is why something is wrong. 

For religion to be formed, the concept of the fall must be clear. Only then can a solid religion be established. You must understand that without the concept of the fall, there is no need for religion. What is the fall? It is unhappiness. Because of the fall, we are fighting against unhappy rocks and all the unhappy barriers. This is the mission of religion: to destroy and overcome these. That is why religion is necessary. Religion must break through this, break through. Do you understand? "Yes." 

So what must religion do? It must fight against unhappiness. To be a religious person means to fight against unhappiness. Then what does it mean to be a religious person? Does it mean centering on a specific person, or if there is a God, centering on God? It must be about believing in God. 

Then, is the God they believe in a happy being or an unhappy being who leads all people through history to walk the path of tears, blood, and sweat? "An unhappy being." 

As we go through our lives, passing through 70, 80, or 100 years, if we walk the path of tears, blood, and sweat, and if there is a providence to overcome the eternal injustice and unhappy environment before us, how sad must God be? How miserable must He be? We must think about this. 

The Fall and God's Sorrow

Now, the fall and God's sorrow… Today, all people in the world say there is no one living like animals, but those who think meaningfully and pursue the true value of humanity… In denying this evil world and pursuing a good world, what can deny this evil world? Is it human strength, or whose strength is it? This is an extremely important question. 

That is why religion is about how to sense the concept of the fall and the resentment of the fall. This determines the weight of faith. Fallen humans may naturally feel this way, but God has also been miserable. How miserable has He been? We must think about the fact that He has been indescribably miserable. 

So is the problem with humanity or with God? That is the question. Is the problem with people or with God? "The problem is with people." If the problem is with people, then there is no need for God. People can solve it without God. If only God is the problem, then there is no need for people. 

So where is the problem? The problem is between God and people, between God and humanity. Therefore, God and people must become one. Since they are in the same position, whatever they resolve, they must have the same heart, the same attitude, and the same actions. 

God is currently shedding tears, but I am laughing. God is climbing the rugged mountains, heading toward the peaks like Mont Blanc, while people are walking on flat ground. People eat three meals a day, having lunch at lunchtime, dinner at dinnertime, breakfast in the morning, sleeping at night, and working when it is time to work. But does God do the same? Does God have times to sleep and eat? Does He manage like that? Is God living within the earth or outside of it? One year, two years—that is a statement within the earth. That is of no use to God. It is the same. 

When you have been sad for a day, does the sadness disappear if someone comforts you? Think about it. If God were in a position to be sad… It is like the story of the ant and the grasshopper; the ant works hard, while the grasshopper just dances, so the ant cannot understand why it is working so hard. The dancing grasshopper does not know the difficulties of the working ant.

Crossing the Border
Most people living in the world probably do not like borders. How about you? "No." If humans feel this way, how does God feel? "God doesn't like them either."

The reason borders arise is that there are different owners.
So, when we examine the history of borders, we must ask who created them. Of course, in the human world, it is centered around humans, so humans created them. However, if there is a God above humans, then we can see that borders between gods began to arise, leading to such things.

If there is a fundamentally good God, and everything is united around that good God, then there are no borders. If that were the case, it would mean that the authority of goodness can only exist where goodness is present.

If there are things that oppose goodness, or if goodness is harmed or obstructed, there will undoubtedly be limitations. This is necessary for protection… Such regulations must exist.

When God created Adam and Eve and placed them in a world of goodness, there must have been a boundary to protect the good Adam and Eve and God Himself. If that state were to be violated, there would be a boundary to limit it. This limitation and protection must occur within the realm of goodness, and not outside of it.

When God told Adam and Eve not to eat from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, it was ultimately for their protection, a boundary. There was one owner in that situation. You must understand this. A good God needed limitations and protection. However, when we speak of borders, you must understand that there are two owners. Therefore, when there are two owners and a boundary is established, that becomes a border.

For example, if there is Belvedere, and there is another owner centered around Belvedere, a border arises there. Everything proceeds in this manner. Additionally, the limitations or protections that say people living here should not fight among themselves are necessary within the community.

When we look at it this way, how many borders exist in each field? Think about how many borders surround us. There are countless countries on this earth. There are countries to the east, countries to the west, and each country goes in a direction 180 degrees apart. In this context, for there to be one owner, these borders must be abolished. If God exists, and if God is the central being, then for God to become one owner, all surrounding borders must be abolished. Only then can there be one owner.

It is true that borders arose because humanity fell. If fallen people had centered everything around God and made efforts to obey and unite, sacrificing everything for God, then many borders would not have arisen.

So how did so many borders come to exist? They emerged from divisions based on personal claims. If there are siblings and parents in one house, and if parents and children fight, invisible borders arise. When siblings fight, invisible borders begin to form.

Only true love can break down borders.
So, how do we carry out the movement to abolish borders? This must be abolished in any case. Should we abolish it by following the side of evil, or by following the side of good? "By following the side of good." To unite around goodness, the direction must change from the side of evil, the opposing side. It changes. Thus, we conclude that there are only two paths: one is to forcibly make unity centered around oneself, and the other is to create unity through obedience. Therefore, in the human world, every person must cross these borders; it is their destiny to cross them. They must cross many borders. Have you felt that? "Yes."

From that perspective, when God comes to our human world, are there no borders? "There are." Even God cannot do as He pleases. If there is a Satan, even Satan cannot do as he pleases. Thus, as our principle states, it is a struggle over one person, a struggle to take that person away.

In this context, the struggle is centered around the individual. The struggle continues to revolve around the individual. So, has the struggle over the individual ended? Do you think it has ended now? "No." Then, if there is a boundary for the individual, do you think there is no boundary for the family? "There is." Oh, that's a big problem. There is a boundary for the family, then there is a boundary for the tribe, then a boundary for the nation, then a boundary for the world, and there are boundaries for heaven and the spirit world. Think about it.

People wish to fight and win against the boundary of the individual, win against the boundary of the family, win against the boundary of the tribe, win against the boundary of the nation, win against the boundary of the world. However, there is not a single person in the world who wants to fight and win against all of them.

From this perspective, what kind of strategy would God have employed to cross borders? Would He have fought? What would He have done? Would He have engaged in violent conflict? Would He have acted forcibly? "No." Then what? "Through obedience and sacrifice." So, what happens when we obey and sacrifice? Then everything is lost. How can we advance from there?

Since the original owner is God, there are covenants in the struggle over these borders, in the struggle to take people away. If there is a law, what is that covenant? That covenant must be an unchanging one. This applies to crossing the boundaries of the individual, family, tribe, nation, and the entire world; that covenant must not be one that changes from time to time. It must be one covenant.

If it is an individual, the individual must be completely united with that covenant; if it is a family, the family must be united; if there are ten people, they must be completely united with the covenant. If there are a hundred people, a thousand people, a tribe, a nation, if the 240 million citizens of America unite with that covenant, they will cross over. Such principles must exist. What is that covenant?

Now, Satan and God, Satan says, "Originally, God is a good God, and I have become an evil god; therefore, I must establish a covenant based on evil content." God says, "I am a good god, so I must establish a covenant based on good content." They are in conflict.

Now, God can assert… God is the owner. Angels are beings created by God. Therefore, they must be under God's dominion. Satan knows this. He knows the principles of existence in the universe. When God and Adam and Eve exist, it is the love that unites Adam and Eve. Furthermore, it is the love meant to unite even the angelic world. It is the love meant to unite the entire created world. Covering up becomes siding with Satan.

The place where you carry the history of honorable love is heaven. Parents must get the grandfather's consent to send their grandchildren anywhere. They cannot do it at their own discretion. The grandfather becomes the position of God. (Pointing to what he wrote) Do you understand what that means? 

In American style, they would really dislike that. When parents are going somewhere and the child says, "I want to go too," they cannot say, "You can’t come! You can’t come!" How can they stop their own child from following them? They would take them along. They cannot stop them because they want to do something else. When a mother is going somewhere and the child says, "I want to go too," they cannot say, "You can’t come." If there is no problem of secrets being revealed, why can’t they let them come?

Now, if a mother is going somewhere and the father-in-law says, "I want to go too," they cannot say, "Just stay back." They would say, "Let’s go." Who can stop them? They cannot stop them. It is good if grandparents, parents, and children all go together. Heaven is like this. You cannot hide from your parents, you cannot hide from your husband or wife, you cannot hide from your grandparents, and you cannot hide from your children. You must understand that the place where you carry the history of honorable love is heaven.

You must become a wife and husband who have love without shame before your in-laws, husband, and children. Then you can enter heaven without any problems. Do you understand what I mean? That is the original world. A family centered on love is such an amazing thing. That is why seeing your sons and daughters makes your eyes happy, your nose happy, your ears happy, your mouth happy, your sense of touch happy, your heart happy, and your spirit happy, and that is happiness. 

When you think like this, if you hear your grandfather cough, "Oh, that guy's..."
"Old man, hurry up and die," they say, and even the sound of grandfather's cough is "Oh, how nice!" Who has the most experience and the longest career in the world? It is the grandfathers and grandmothers. Because they are old, they don’t sleep. Think about that. "Wow, our grandfather is like God, watching over us without sleeping! He has aged because he protects us. Looking at his wrinkles, he has aged..." You should think like that. Therefore, you must absolutely obey the commands. How beautiful is that? If you serve such grandfathers and grandmothers, there will be no fires and no theft. You must understand this.

What do grandfathers and grandmothers do when they don’t sleep? They pray. They pray, "God, please bless our sons and daughters." Because they pray, they teach us, "Hey, be careful today! It’s dangerous out there. Listen to me." They say, "Don’t go out today! Don’t fight! Son, don’t go anywhere, daughter! Daughter-in-law! Don’t go far today." They teach us like this. (Laughter)

Those who try to live in the ideal original form are protected by the universe. So, don’t you think grandsons need such grandfathers and grandmothers? When there is love, grandmothers and grandfathers dance, mothers and fathers dance, and siblings dance. Think about it. If everyone is dancing disco at home and then they all fall down and wet themselves, would God punish them? Even if they wet themselves 24 hours a day, God would say, "Wow, that’s cool!" (Laughter)

If this is a hypothetical statement, then the reality is even more plausible, but is that really the case? You must understand that reality is more than the ideal. The person who tries to live in this way will be protected by the universe. If someone tries to kill that person, the universe will automatically protect them.

So, Reverend Moon is dignified even though the country and the world oppose him. Do you like someone like me? "Yes." I like you too. Do you want to try being like me? "Yes." That is the ideal original form. Now, young people today don’t like grandfathers and grandmothers going to nursing homes, right? "No." In the Unification Church, we should say, "Abolish all that, stop it," and then it will automatically disappear, right? "Automatically." Then will that home become a paradise for grandfathers and grandmothers? Will it become a paradise for grandmothers and grandfathers, or not? "It will." What about mothers and fathers? And the sons and daughters? "It will become a paradise."

Today, the American system is a paradise for young people, not for grandfathers and grandmothers. It is not a paradise for children, nor for grandfathers and grandmothers; it is a paradise for young men and women, which is why it is all digging a pit of hell. Why? Because it does not match the original form. What is a trash can? It is a container for disposing of things that deviate from their original state, and the world of human trash is hell. 

Now, do you understand what I mean? "Yes." From nature to family, God created the world centered on love because God is also seeking love. Because He has not found that love, this providential history continues until now, moving toward eternity until that love is found. Think about whether it is a sad thing or a joyful thing for God that the Unification Church has come out and revealed such facts. What do you think? "It is a joyful thing."

Grandmothers and grandfathers should be able to enter their sons' and daughters' rooms at any time, day or night, without boundaries. The same goes for sons and daughters. Sons and daughters should feel free to enter their mothers' and fathers' rooms at midnight or one o'clock, and mothers and fathers should feel happy when grandmothers and grandfathers come into their rooms, and sons and daughters should feel happy when their mothers and fathers come into their rooms. If a grandson goes to his grandfather's room to eat something, he should be told, "Go ahead and eat." He should also be able to eat if he finds something in his mother's room. He should be able to eat if he finds something in his children's room. He should also be able to eat in his daughter-in-law's room. He should be able to eat freely, sleep freely, and play freely. (Laughter)

In American families, when grandfathers go to their sons' houses, they call ahead. What would a person prefer? What would you prefer? Look. If a beautiful daughter-in-law, with a loving heart, wants to buy something better for her beloved husband than for the gray-haired grandfathers and grandmothers, how beautiful and lovely would that be? If a pretty daughter-in-law, despite her old grandfather and grandmother being wrinkled, buys something for her beloved husband with more joy than anything else, how wonderful would that scene be? Then, all that grandfathers and grandmothers have hidden... they give all their love.

Inheriting the original love means fulfilling all responsibilities in the world. Now, who is the oldest grandfather in the world? "God." That’s right. (Laughter) So, learning to love that grandfather is learning from your own grandfather. By learning this tradition, I can receive all the love treasures from God’s grandfather's secret storehouse. How wonderful is that? Then your ancestors will take you before God and boast, saying, "Our grandson lived like this." Moreover, the ancestors above will say, "You are the best. You are the best," and send you before God. Then God will say, "Such sons and daughters must be blessed. They must receive blessings." "Your family will never perish. You will receive blessings forever." Do you think God would do that? "I think so." Reverend Moon thinks like that.

When I meet a grandfather on the street, it is still the same. So, when you meet a grandfather, you might feel hungry because you have no money and you might want to buy him something delicious. You should think, "I should treat him like my grandfather," and think of older people like your own parents, and if they are younger, think of them like your grandchildren, your daughters, and your sons. You should eliminate boundaries. Do you understand? "Yes." A person who lives like that will surely... that is the ideal love nest of the original form. Do you understand? Do you want to try living like that? "Yes." When you go to the Alps, think from that perspective, "Ah, this world is high. There is snow on the mountains, and flowers are blooming. Ah, there is a green hill. Ah, how nice."

I want you to think that I am traveling through the world created by God instead of God. I want you to appreciate everything related to love before God. This nature is a zoo of original beings, a garden of original beings, a park of original beings. Do you understand what I mean? Even when going through the desert, you should not think it is scary. Do you understand what I mean?

You must always feel that the pursuit of such an ideal family, a country based on such a family, a world centered on such a country, and a heaven centered on such a world is directly connected to you. Now, do you want to live like that? "Yes." How affectionate a person is, how... Even if you are tired there, you will gain the strength to go on with love. Even if you die while drawing love, you will die in love. The teacher also had this dream and met his mother, and that is how they became one. That is why we call such people happy. Do you want to try? "Yes."

Being good at speaking, doing things well, and being good at everything is not as important as inheriting this original love, which allows you to fulfill all responsibilities in the world. Then the teacher will surely welcome you with joy, and God will surely welcome you with joy.

In the spirit world, you will live with love that can be enjoyed forever. So, what will you do in the spirit world? You will sing songs of love and speak with love. In the spirit world, if someone sings over there, in other words, if they speak operatically over there, I must respond operatically. If they speak with dance, I must respond with dance. (Laughter) Even if you dance forever, you will never get tired of it. When one place dances, heaven dances all together, and when one place sings, everyone sings together. At that time, you will dance with your beloved wife. If you dance with someone else's woman, you will think, "Ah, I am dancing with you to love my beloved wife a hundred times more than I love you." If you hold hands and dance with someone else's woman, it is all to stimulate a thousand or ten thousand times more love for your beloved.

Do you need to work in the spirit world? Do you have to work eight hours there? "No." Is there night? There is no night. You are always awake. All these organs are working, but what are they doing? What are they doing? What kind of work can you do while being awake forever and never sleeping? It is love. (Laughter) If you just have that love, when you say, "Hey, come out!" it will come out immediately. If ten thousand people gather here and say, "Prepare ten thousand meals and tables!" it will be prepared immediately. (Laughter)

If you take love out of it, what is there to talk about? How will you live? (Laughter) How can you live with a heart full of dislike? There, you live with love, centered on original love. Reverend Moon knows such a world, so no matter how difficult things are in the world, he can overcome them, and he can cut off good things as well. He can cut off things that ordinary people cannot. He cuts them off completely. Do you understand what I mean? We take that as a standard and measure our progress.

That is why you like Reverend Moon. How many hours have I talked? It’s almost five hours. Even after talking like this, it is not boring... Five hours is the time it takes to fly from New York to San Francisco, and how boring is that? (Laughter) Reverend Moon talks for five hours; how long is that? How long is that? Talking about this and hearing this, how much... (Laughter) That is because love is here.

So, did you do well to join the Unification Church, or not? "I did well." Now, whatever I do, will you be grateful if I train you accordingly? "Yes." Will you not complain? "Yes." A person who complains cannot be a true person. If someone has suffered in the Unification Church, who has suffered the most? The teacher has suffered the most. And who has suffered more between God and the teacher? "God." That is why I have no complaints about God. Do you have complaints about me? "No." (Laughter) That is love. If someone curses you, it may hurt your heart, but if the teacher curses you, it does not hurt your heart. That is because love is involved in it, love. Even if you are beaten, if there is love, you will like it. Do you want to walk that path? "Yes." How many years do you want to walk? "Forever." Forever. You are forever seeking it. Only on this earth can this be shortened. In the spirit world, because it is a stimulating world centered on love, once it is bound, there is no place to untie it. You must untie everything before you go. You must untie everything before you go.

Now, today is June 8th, and you shall head straight to the world of love in its original state! Amen! "Amen!" (Applause) *
